 pehle samajhate hai ki yah bill he kya
 a new law was proposed in India in 2010 to replace the law that had been in operation since 1957, but that proposal could not become a law until 2014

 a
 1 kahata he ki is kanoon ke banane ke baad mining se judi sari puraani arziyaan cancil ho jaaegi

 The upsurge in Wimbledon's third Grand Slam tournament this year continued on Wednesday, and this time it was the defending champion and third-seeded world record holder Roger Federer, after Rafael Nadal, Layton Hewitt, Maria Sharapova, Anna Ivanovich and Sarah Irani
 saat baar vimbledon main purush ekal khitaab jeet chuke roger federer ko yah jhelana padaa ukraine ke 116veen variyata praapt 27-varshiya khilaadi sargei stakhovski ke haathon, jisane federer par duusare daur main teen ghante tak khinche marathon mukaable ke dauraan 6-7 (5-7), 7-6 (7-5), 7-5, 7-6 (7-5) se jeet hasil kii
 Roger Federer has previously reached the quarter-finals of Grand Slam tournaments for 36 consecutive times, and finished out of a Grand Slam before making it to the final eight for the first time since the 2004 French Open
 sargei stakhovski se haar jane ke baad swiss champion ne kaha, "main behad niraash hum
